The HR department has previously supplemented the gender- disaggregated pay sta- tistics with more in -depth analyses, where pay is also related to other factors such as seniority and business performance. These analyses have greatly reduced unexplained pay gaps. In 2025, wage transparency will be one of the Bank’s focus areas, which is expected to increase insight into any unexplained pay gaps. The gender pay gap is calculated as the differ- ence of average pay levels between male and fe- male employees, expressed as a percentage of the average pay level of male employees. The pay gap is calculated solely on the basis of gender. This does not take into account job functions, sen- iority, skills, etc., which are important factors in ensuring equal pay for work of the same kind or equal value.   • Follow -up and reporting on well -being goals takes place annually from the HR department to the Bank’s Executive Board and Board of Directors. Target for the under-represented gender In order to achieve an equal gender diversity in Spar Nord’s management, including the Board of Directors, the Nomination and Remuneration Com- mittee has set targets for the under- represented gender, which have been approved by the Board of Directors. The t argets include statutory targets for the Board of Directors and other management levels as well as voluntary targets for the Execu- tive Board, the group of executive managers and managers. Follow -up and reporting on targets for the under -represented gender takes place annu- ally from the Executive Board to the Nomination and Remuneration Committee and the Board of Di-rectors. The gender diversity in the Bank’s total workforce is largely equal between women and men, whereas women constitute the under -represented gender in the Bank’s management. XX

Quel est le ratio de rémunération totale annuelle au sein de l'entreprise ? Quel est le montant total de la rémunération annuelle pour les employés (y compris les salaires, les primes, les avantages et autres compensations)



Pour répondre à cette question, merci de fournir :

Le montant total de la rémunération annuelle pour les employés (y compris les salaires, les primes, les avantages et autres compensations).
Des détails sur la méthodologie utilisée pour calculer ce ratio, y compris les critères pris en compte.
Si disponible, des informations sur l'évolution de ce ratio au fil des années, ainsi que des comparaisons avec des normes sectorielles ou des benchmarks.

Je ne dispose pas des informations spécifiques concernant le montant total de la rémunération annuelle pour les employés, y compris les salaires, les primes, les avantages et autres compensations. Cependant, je peux vous fournir des détails sur le ratio de rémunération.

Le ratio de rémunération est calculé comme le rapport entre la rémunération totale annuelle du PDG (l'individu le mieux rémunéré de l'entreprise) et la médiane de la rémunération annuelle totale des autres employés de la banque, à l'exclusion du PDG. En 2024, ce ratio a augmenté à 10,2, par rapport à 9,6 en 2023 (Context Num-3).

Ce ratio permet d'évaluer l'écart de rémunération entre le PDG et les employés moyens, mais je n'ai pas d'informations sur l'évolution de ce ratio au fil des années antérieures à 2023 ou de comparaisons avec des normes sectorielles. Pour des informations plus détaillées sur les montants spécifiques ou des comparaisons sectorielles, il serait nécessaire de consulter des sources supplémentaires ou les documents financiers officiels de l'entreprise.

    - Conseil d'administration exécutif : Composé uniquement d'hommes, avec une proportion de 100 %. - Groupe des cadres dirigeants : Sur un total de 57 personnes, 9 sont des femmes (16 %) et 48 sont des hommes (84 %). - Managers : Sur un total de 160 personnes, 52 sont des femmes (33 %) et 108 sont des hommes (67 %).
    La proportion de femmes augmente progressivement dans les catégories professionnelles inférieures.

Je suis désolé, mais les documents fournis ne contiennent pas d'informations spécifiques sur le montant total de la rémunération annuelle pour les employés de l'entreprise, y compris les salaires, les primes, les avantages et autres compensations. De plus, aucun détail sur la méthodologie utilisée pour calculer le ratio de rémunération totale annuelle ni des comparaisons avec des normes sectorielles ou des benchmarks n'est mentionné dans les contextes disponibles.

Los grupos internos incluyen el Consejo de Administración, la Junta Ejecutiva, el grupo de dirección ESG, el Comité de Inversión Responsable, el Comité de Finanzas Sostenibles y los empleados, con actividades como reuniones trimestrales, talleres y consultas, enfocadas en metas de sostenibilidad, gobernanza y desarrollo de productos responsables.   • ### Pay gap between the CEO and employees The pay gap between the CEO and employees, which is also referred to as the remuneration ratio, is calculated as the ratio between the annual to- tal remuneration of the CEO (the company's high- est paid individual) and the median of the Bank's annual total remuneration (excluding the highest paid individual).
  • The table titled "Compensation metrics" compares data for the years 2024 and 2023. It includes two rows: "Gender pay gap (%)" and "Remuneration ratio (ratio)." The "Gender pay gap (%)" decreased from 22.6% in 2023 to 21.4% in 2024. The "Remuneration ratio (ratio)" increased from 9.6 in 2023 to 10.2 in 2024.
  • ### END TABLE The gender pay gap is calculated as the differ- ence of average pay levels between male and fe- male employees, expressed as a percentage of the average pay level of male employees. The pay gap is calculated solely on the basis of gender. This does not take into account job functions, sen- iority, skills, etc., which are important factors in ensuring equal pay for work of the same kind or equal value. The remuneration ratio shows the ratio between remuneration of the Bank's highest paid individual (the CEO) and the median remuneration of the Bank's other employees.
  • ### Pay The starting point is a calculated full-time monthly salary consisting of monthly salary, sup- plements, employer-paid pension including ATP, bonus/lump sum, tax value of employee benefits and holiday allowance.
  • ### Staff turnover rate Staff turnover is calculated for employees leaving voluntarily and involuntarily (excluding employ- ees with temporary contracts and temps) who left the company during the year relative to the aver- age number of employees in 2024. Employee turn- over is measured as a percentage.
  • The table titled "Employees Number (FTEs)" presents data for the years 2024, 2023, and 2022. It shows that the "Number of employees (year-end)" increased from 1,644 in 2022 to 1,703 in 2023, and further to 1,750 in 2024. Similarly, the "Number of employees (average)" rose from 1,628 in 2022 to 1,664 in 2023, and then to 1,721 in 2024.
  • ### Gender diversity for management levels Number of women in relation to the total number of managers at each management layer. Other management layers include the Executive Board and managers with HR responsibilities who report directly to the Executive Board. Gender diversity at management levels is calculated as a percentage.
  • ### Pay difference between genders The difference of average pay levels between male and female employees, expressed as a per- centage of the average pay level of male employ- ees. The pay difference between genders is calcu- lated as a percentage.

Je suis désolé, mais je ne peux pas fournir le montant total de la rémunération annuelle pour les employés car cette information spécifique n'est pas incluse dans les documents fournis. Cependant, je peux partager des détails sur le ratio de rémunération, qui est disponible dans les contextes.

Le ratio de rémunération, également appelé ratio de rémunération, est calculé comme le rapport entre la rémunération totale annuelle du PDG (la personne la mieux rémunérée de l'entreprise) et la rémunération médiane annuelle des autres employés de la banque. En 2023, ce ratio était de 9,6 et il a augmenté à 10,2 en 2024.

La méthodologie pour calculer ce ratio prend en compte la rémunération totale du PDG et la rémunération médiane des employés, à l'exclusion de la personne la mieux rémunérée. Cela inclut les salaires, les primes, les avantages et autres compensations.

Je n'ai pas d'informations sur l'évolution de ce ratio sur d'autres années ou des comparaisons avec des normes sectorielles ou des benchmarks.

S1-173

Quel est le ratio de la rémunération annuelle totale de la personne la mieux payée par rapport à la rémunération totale annuelle médiane de tous les salariés (à l'exclusion de la personne la mieux rémunérée) au sein de l'entreprise ?

nan

Le ratio de la rémunération annuelle totale de la personne la mieux payée (le CEO) par rapport à la rémunération totale annuelle médiane de tous les salariés (à l'exclusion de la personne la mieux rémunérée) est de 10,2 en 2024.

    Le tableau présente la répartition des femmes et des hommes dans trois catégories professionnelles en 2024 : le conseil d'administration exécutif, le groupe des cadres dirigeants et les managers.
    - Conseil d'administration exécutif : Composé uniquement d'hommes, avec une proportion de 100 %. - Groupe des cadres dirigeants : Sur un total de 57 personnes, 9 sont des femmes (16 %) et 48 sont des hommes (84 %). - Managers : Sur un total de 160 personnes, 52 sont des femmes (33 %) et 108 sont des hommes (67 %).
    La proportion de femmes augmente progressivement dans les catégories professionnelles inférieures.

Both permanent and temporary em- ployees are included in the calculation. Gender di- versity is measured as a percentage.   • La tabla presenta temas de sostenibilidad relacionados con la cadena de valor, una descripción de impacto, riesgo y medidas políticas entre los años indicados. Los temas incluyen "Cultura corporativa" con impacto positivo en "Operaciones propias" y medidas como la "Política sobre cultura corporativa"; "Protección de denunciantes" con impacto positivo en "Operaciones propias" y la "Política de denunciantes"; y "Gestión de relaciones con proveedores" con impacto positivo en "Upstream" y medidas como "Documentos y procesos de gobernanza".   • La tabla detalla la organización y resultados del compromiso de Spar Nord con grupos de interés internos y externos en 2024. Los grupos internos incluyen el Consejo de Administración, la Junta Ejecutiva, el grupo de dirección ESG, el Comité de Inversión Responsable, el Comité de Finanzas Sostenibles y los empleados, con actividades como reuniones trimestrales, talleres y consultas, enfocadas en metas de sostenibilidad, gobernanza y desarrollo de productos responsables. Los grupos externos abarcan clientes empresariales y minoristas, proveedores, accionistas, grupos industriales, asociaciones y la comunidad local, con iniciativas como encuestas, diálogos, productos sostenibles y reportes anuales alineados con principios de la ONU. Los resultados incluyen la integración de sostenibilidad en procesos de inversión, financiamiento verde, cumplimiento de códigos de conducta y apoyo a transformaciones sostenibles. Las metas están vinculadas a ESRS E1 y S1, y se alinean con la estrategia y modelo de negocio del banco.
  • ### Pay gap between the CEO and employees The pay gap between the CEO and employees, which is also referred to as the remuneration ratio, is calculated as the ratio between the annual to- tal remuneration of the CEO (the company's high- est paid individual) and the median of the Bank's annual total remuneration (excluding the highest paid individual).
  • The table titled "Compensation metrics" compares data for the years 2024 and 2023. It includes two rows: "Gender pay gap (%)" and "Remuneration ratio (ratio)." The "Gender pay gap (%)" decreased from 22.6% in 2023 to 21.4% in 2024. The "Remuneration ratio (ratio)" increased from 9.6 in 2023 to 10.2 in 2024.
  • ### END TABLE The gender pay gap is calculated as the differ- ence of average pay levels between male and fe- male employees, expressed as a percentage of the average pay level of male employees. The pay gap is calculated solely on the basis of gender. This does not take into account job functions, sen- iority, skills, etc., which are important factors in ensuring equal pay for work of the same kind or equal value. The remuneration ratio shows the ratio between remuneration of the Bank's highest paid individual (the CEO) and the median remuneration of the Bank's other employees.
  • ### Gender diversity for management levels Number of women in relation to the total number of managers at each management layer. Other management layers include the Executive Board and managers with HR responsibilities who report directly to the Executive Board. Gender diversity at management levels is calculated as a percentage.
  • ### Pay difference between genders The difference of average pay levels between male and female employees, expressed as a per- centage of the average pay level of male employ- ees. The pay difference between genders is calcu- lated as a percentage.
  • ## Financial reporting developments across different job functions. In ad- dition, the Nomination and Remuneration Commit- tee is informed. The HR department has previously supplemented the gender-disaggregated pay sta- tistics with more in-depth analyses, where pay is also related to other factors such as seniority and business performance. These analyses have greatly reduced unexplained pay gaps. In 2025, wage transparency will be one of the Bank's focus areas, which is expected to increase insight into any unexplained pay gaps.
  • ### Pay difference between genders Ensuring equal pay for work of the same kind or work of equal value is one of the basic elements of Spar Nord's remuneration policy. The Bank's joint consultation committee annually reviews gender- disaggregated pay statistics in order to monitor Spar Nord Annual Report 2024 93
  • ### Staff turnover rate Staff turnover is calculated for employees leaving voluntarily and involuntarily (excluding employ- ees with temporary contracts and temps) who left the company during the year relative to the aver- age number of employees in 2024. Employee turn- over is measured as a percentage.

Le ratio de la rémunération annuelle totale de la personne la mieux payée par rapport à la rémunération totale annuelle médiane de tous les salariés (à l'exclusion de la personne la mieux rémunérée) est appelé le "remuneration ratio". Selon le contexte fourni, ce ratio a augmenté de 9,6 en 2023 à 10,2 en 2024.

  • the Bank are based on baseline analyses of the Bank’s climate footprint through scope 1, 2 and 3. As the Bank’s climate change initiatives are an on- going process, the baseline years are not identical across the three impact areas. However, the 2050 ambition is shared across the entire business, just as all activities have been assigned sub -targets for decarbonisation by 2030. Spar Nord’s targets have been substantiated using scientific scenarios, which are de scribed in more detail under the spe- cific activity. The reduction targets for financed emissions from the Bank’s core activities of loans and investments relate to significant shares of the Bank’s business volume for bank and leasing loans and invest- ments in equities and corporate bonds in the Bank’s asset management. Incidents, complaints and human rights In 2024, no complaints were filed, and no in- stances of discriminatory treatment or violations, including harassment, were recorded in the Bank’s own workforce. Similarly, there were no incidents with a material impact on human rights or com- plaints related to such matters. The Bank has a response plan in place to handle discrimination and violations, should such inci- dents arise. The HR department initiates the response plan and involves relevant parties, in- cluding the management and the union repre- sentative. Each employee is supported individu-ally, and the necessary assistance is provided. For the sake of the employee, discretion is exercised. In addition, the j oint consultation committee annu- ally discusses the Bank’s guidelines and status in this area with a view to ensuring an effective re- sponse plan. Working condi- tions and remuneration are regulated by the standard collective agreement for all employees.
